## Exercise 1
1:
$$
V_{AB} = (-2, 4, -4), V_{AD} = (-4, 3, 0)
$$
2:
$$
C = A + V_{AB} + V_{AD} = (-4, 10, 0)
$$
$$
3: Given: V_{AB}, V_{AD}
$$
Parallelogram: Equal opposite sides; 
$$
U = \sqrt{4+16+16}*2+\sqrt{16} 
$$
$$
C = A + V_{AB} + V_{AD} = ((-4, 10, 0)+ 9 + 0)*2 = 12 + 10 = 22 LU
$$
4: 
$$
V_AC = (-8, 4, -8); d_AC = sqrt(64 + 16 + 64) = 12 LU
$$
WRONG
